  <script type="text/javascript">
   function ADS_setup() {
	var ad_slots = window.ad_slots || [];
	googletag.cmd.push(function() {
		var slot_BH = googletag.defineSlot('/1049606/ca-pub-6063938032580800-tag/outdooractive_desktop_start_skyscraper', [[300, 600], [160, 600], [120, 600]], 'BH').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting("userLevel", "none").setTargeting("language", "en");
if (slot_BH) {
	ad_slots.push(slot_BH);
}

var slot_AH = googletag.defineSlot('/1049606/ca-pub-6063938032580800-tag/outdooractive_desktop_start_leaderboard', [[800, 250], [970, 250], [728, 90], [1079, 180], [842, 250]], 'AH').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting("userLevel", "none").setTargeting("language", "en");
if (slot_AH) {
	ad_slots.push(slot_AH);
}

var slot_HO = googletag.defineSlot('/1049606/ca-pub-6063938032580800-tag/outdooractive_desktop_start_rectangle', [300, 250], 'HO').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting("userLevel", "none").setTargeting("language", "en");
if (slot_HO) {
	ad_slots.push(slot_HO);
}

var slot_FO = googletag.defineSlot('/1049606/ca-pub-6063938032580800-tag/outdooractive_desktop_start_footerad', [[728, 90], [728, 180], [770, 250], [800, 250], [800, 600], [970, 250]], 'FO').addService(googletag.pubads()).setTargeting("userLevel", "none").setTargeting("language", "en");
if (slot_FO) {
	ad_slots.push(slot_FO);
}


	
		googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true);
		googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
		googletag.pubads().enableVideoAds();
		googletag.pubads().setCentering(true);
		
		if (!oa.cookie.hasConsent('personalisation')) {
			googletag.pubads().setRequestNonPersonalizedAds(1);
		}
		
        googletag.pubads().enableLazyLoad({
           // Fetch slots within 2 viewports.
           fetchMarginPercent: 200,
           // Render slots within 1 viewports.
           renderMarginPercent: 100,
           // Double the above values on mobile, where viewports are smaller
           // and users tend to scroll faster.
           mobileScaling: 2.0
        });
        
		googletag.enableServices();
	});

	googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('BH'); });
googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('AH'); });
googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('HO'); });

}
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   window.addEventListener("load",function () {
     _check_oa();
     function _check_oa() {
       if (typeof oa === "undefined"  ||  oa  &&  typeof oa.api === "undefined")
         setTimeout( _check_oa, 345 );
       else
       {
          var _oaxApp = typeof dp !== "undefined"  ?  dp
            :  typeof fvp !== "undefined"  ?  fvp
            :  oa._dp  ||  oa._fvp
            ;
		if (_oaxApp)
			_oaxApp.whenLoaded( alp.asyncF( 1000, function() {
			_oaxApp.overlayChangeEvt().then( onOverlayChangeEvent );
			function onOverlayChangeEvent(overlay) {
				if (!overlay) {
					alp.m( alp.m( alp.sub( 'googletag' ), 'pubads' ), 'refresh' );
					alp.m( alp.sub( 'iom' ), 'c', alp.sub('iam_data'), 1 );
				}
			};
		}));
                }
                }
	});
  </script>
